decoder.layers.39.self_attn.k_proj
decoder.layers.39.self_attn.v_proj
decoder.layers.39.self_attn.q_proj
decoder.layers.39.self_attn.out_proj
decoder.layers.39.self_attn.bmm1
decoder.layers.39.self_attn.bmm2
decoder.layers.39.activation_fn
decoder.layers.39.self_attn_layer_norm
decoder.layers.39.fc1
decoder.layers.39.fc2
decoder.layers.39.final_layer_norm
OPTForCausalLM(
  (model): OPTModel(
    (decoder): OPTDecoder(
      (embed_tokens): Embedding(50272, 5120, padding_idx=1)
      (embed_positions): OPTLearnedPositionalEmbedding(2050, 5120)
      (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (layers): ModuleList(
        (0): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0)
            (v_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0)
            (q_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0)
            (out_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=None, err_prob=0.0)
            (bmm1): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0)
            (bmm2): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0)
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 20480, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0)
          (fc2): NoisyW8A8Linear(20480, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (1): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (v_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (out_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (bmm1): TorchBMM()
            (bmm2): TorchBMM()
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=20480, bias=True)
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=20480, out_features=5120, bias=True)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (2): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (v_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (out_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (bmm1): TorchBMM()
            (bmm2): TorchBMM()
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()

  (model): OPTModel(
    (decoder): OPTDecoder(
      (embed_tokens): Embedding(50272, 5120, padding_idx=1)
      (embed_positions): OPTLearnedPositionalEmbedding(2050, 5120)
      (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (layers): ModuleList(
        (0): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-08)
            (v_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-08)
            (q_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-08)
            (out_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=None, err_prob=1e-08)
            (bmm1): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-08)
            (bmm2): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-08)
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 20480, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-08)
          (fc2): NoisyW8A8Linear(20480, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-08)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (1): OPTDecoderLayer(

OPTForCausalLM(
  (model): OPTModel(
    (decoder): OPTDecoder(
      (embed_tokens): Embedding(50272, 5120, padding_idx=1)
      (embed_positions): OPTLearnedPositionalEmbedding(2050, 5120)
      (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (layers): ModuleList(
        (0): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-07)
            (v_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-07)
            (q_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-07)
            (out_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=None, err_prob=1e-07)
            (bmm1): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-07)
            (bmm2): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-07)
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 20480, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-07)
          (fc2): NoisyW8A8Linear(20480, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-07)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (1): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (v_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (out_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (bmm1): TorchBMM()
            (bmm2): TorchBMM()
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=20480, bias=True)
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=20480, out_features=5120, bias=True)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (2): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (v_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (out_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (bmm1): TorchBMM()
            (bmm2): TorchBMM()
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=20480, bias=True)
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=20480, out_features=5120, bias=True)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (3): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (v_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (out_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)

            (bmm2): TorchBMM()
          )

          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)

          (fc2): Linear(in_features=20480, out_features=5120, bias=True)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)

OPTForCausalLM(
  (model): OPTModel(
    (decoder): OPTDecoder(
      (embed_tokens): Embedding(50272, 5120, padding_idx=1)
      (embed_positions): OPTLearnedPositionalEmbedding(2050, 5120)
      (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (layers): ModuleList(
        (0): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-05)
            (v_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-05)
            (q_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-05)
            (out_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=None, err_prob=1e-05)
            (bmm1): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-05)
            (bmm2): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-05)
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 20480, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-05)
          (fc2): NoisyW8A8Linear(20480, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=1e-05)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (1): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (v_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (out_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (bmm1): TorchBMM()
            (bmm2): TorchBMM()

          (fc1): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=20480, bias=True)

)

OPTForCausalLM(
  (model): OPTModel(
    (decoder): OPTDecoder(
      (embed_tokens): Embedding(50272, 5120, padding_idx=1)
      (embed_positions): OPTLearnedPositionalEmbedding(2050, 5120)
      (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (layers): ModuleList(
        (0): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0001)
            (v_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0001)
            (q_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0001)
            (out_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=None, err_prob=0.0001)
            (bmm1): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0001)
            (bmm2): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0001)
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 20480, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0001)
          (fc2): NoisyW8A8Linear(20480, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.0001)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (1): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (v_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (out_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (bmm1): TorchBMM()
            (bmm2): TorchBMM()
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)

  (model): OPTModel(
    (decoder): OPTDecoder(
      (embed_tokens): Embedding(50272, 5120, padding_idx=1)
      (embed_positions): OPTLearnedPositionalEmbedding(2050, 5120)
      (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (layers): ModuleList(
        (0): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.001)
            (v_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.001)
            (q_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.001)
            (out_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=None, err_prob=0.001)
            (bmm1): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.001)
            (bmm2): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.001)
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 20480, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.001)
          (fc2): NoisyW8A8Linear(20480, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.001)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (1): OPTDecoderLayer(

OPTForCausalLM(
  (model): OPTModel(
    (decoder): OPTDecoder(
      (embed_tokens): Embedding(50272, 5120, padding_idx=1)
      (embed_positions): OPTLearnedPositionalEmbedding(2050, 5120)
      (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (layers): ModuleList(
        (0): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.01)
            (v_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.01)
            (q_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.01)
            (out_proj): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=None, err_prob=0.01)
            (bmm1): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.01)
            (bmm2): NoisyW8A8BMM(act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.01)
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): NoisyW8A8Linear(5120, 20480, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.01)
          (fc2): NoisyW8A8Linear(20480, 5120, bias=True, weight_quant=per_tensor, act_quant=per_tensor, output_quant=per_tensor, err_prob=0.01)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (1): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (v_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (out_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (bmm1): TorchBMM()
            (bmm2): TorchBMM()
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=20480, bias=True)
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=20480, out_features=5120, bias=True)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (2): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (v_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (out_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (bmm1): TorchBMM()
            (bmm2): TorchBMM()
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=20480, bias=True)
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=20480, out_features=5120, bias=True)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (3): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (v_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (out_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
            (bmm1): TorchBMM()
            (bmm2): TorchBMM()
          )
          (activation_fn): ReLU()
          (self_attn_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
          (fc1): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=20480, bias=True)
          (fc2): Linear(in_features=20480, out_features=5120, bias=True)
          (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((5120,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        )
        (4): OPTDecoderLayer(
          (self_attn): OPTAttention(
            (k_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)

            (q_proj): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=5120, bias=True)
